 28 sitambar ko lata ji apane jivan ke 84 saal puure kar rahi hai

 madhya pradesh ke indore main 28 sitambar 1929 ko janmin kumari lata deenanath mangeshkar rangamanchi gayak deenanath mangeshkar or sudhamati kii putree hai
 Lata, the eldest of four siblings, started her music training at the age of five
 bahanon aashaa, usha or minaa ke saath sangeet kii shiksha grahan karne ke saath saath lata bachapan se hi rangamanch ke kshetra main bhi sakriy thim
 When Lata was seven years old, her family moved to Mumbai, so she was raised in Mumbai
 varsh 1942 main dil kaa daura padane se pita ke dehavasan ke baad lata ne parivaar ke bharan poshan ke liye kuch varshon tak hindi or marathi filmon main kaam kiya, jinamein pramukh hai 'mira bai', 'paheli mangalagaur' 'maanjhe bal' 'gaja bhaau' 'chhimukala sansar' 'badi maa' 'jivan yatra' or 'chhatrapati shivaji'
 But Lata's destination was singing and music
 bachapan se hi unhen gane kaa shauk tha or sangeet main unki dilchaspee thi
 Lata once told the BBC in a conversation that when she was four-five years old, she used to stand on the cooking stool in the kitchen and recite songs to her mother
 tab tak unke pita ko unke gane ke shauk ke bare main pataa nahin tha
 Once in his father's absence, Lata was explaining to one of his disciples by singing a song, then the father arrived
 pitaaji ne unki maa se kaha, hamaare khud ke ghar main gavaiya baithi he or ham baahar waalon ko sangeet sikhaa rahe hai
 The next day, Dad woke Lata to six o'clock and gave him a tanpura
 lata ke filmon main parshvagayan kii shuruyaat 1942 main marathi film 'kiti hasaal' se hui, lekin durbhaagya se yah geet film main shaamil nahin kiya gaya
 It is said that the road to success is not easy
 lata ko bhi cinema jagat main kariyar ke shuruaati dinon main kaaphi sangharsh karnaa padaa
 Due to his thin voice, musicians initially refused to sing him in films
 apni lagan or pratibha ke bal par haalanki dhire-dhire unhen kaam or pahchaan donon milane lage
 Lata got a big success with the song sung in the 1947 film Aapka Seva Mein and then she did not look back
 varsh 1949 main geet 'aayega aane vaala', 1960 main 'o sajnaa barkhaa bahaar ai', 1958 main 'aajaa re paradesi', 1961 main 'itnaa na tu mujhase pyaar badha', 'allaah tero naam', 'ehsaan tera hoga mujh par' or 1965 main 'ye samaa, samaa he ye pyaar kaa' jaise geeton ke saath unke prashansakon or unki aawaaj ke chaahane waalon kii sankhya lagaataar badhati gai
 It would not be wrong to say that Lata Mangeshkar is another name for singing in Hindi cinema

 Kumari Lata Dinanath Mangeshkar, born on 28 September 1929 in Indore, Madhya Pradesh, is the daughter of theatrical singer Dinanath Mangeshkar and Sudhamati
 chaar bhai-bahanon main sabase badi lata ko unke pita ne paanch saal kii umr se hi sangeet kii talim dilvaani shuru kii thi
 Along with sisters Asha, Usha and Meena, Lata was also active in theater since childhood
 jab lata saat saal kii thim, tab unka parivaar mumbai aa gaya, isliye unki parvarish mumbai main hui
 After the death of her father from a heart attack in 1942, Lata worked in Hindi and Marathi films for a few years to support the family, among which are 'meera Bai', 'paheli Mangalagaur' 'manjhe Bal' Gaja Bhau '' Chhimukala Sansar '' Elder Mother '' Jeevan Yatra '' and 'chhatrapati Shivaji'
 lekin lata kii manzil to gayan or sangeet hi the
 He was fond of singing since childhood and was interested in music
 lata ne ek baar baatcheet main bibisi ko bataaya tha ki jab vah chaar-paanch saal kii thim to kichan main khaanaa banaati stool par khadey hokar apni maa ko gane sunaaya karti thim
 Till then his father did not know about his passion for singing
 ek baar pita kii anupasthiti main unke ek shagird ko lata ek geet ke sur gaakar samajha rahi thim, tabhi pita aa gaye
 Dad said to his mother, Gawiya is sitting in our own house and we are teaching music to outsiders
 agle din pitaaji ne lata ko subah chah baje jagaakar tanpura thama diya
 The playback singing of Lata's films began in 1942 with the Marathi film Keeti Hasal, but unfortunately the song was not included in the film
 kehete hai, safalataa kii raah aasaan nahin hoti
 Lata also had to struggle a lot in the early days of her career in cinema

 However, on the strength of his passion and talent, gradually he started getting both work and recognition
